Player_Black (to Proxy):

make_move d7e6


The position is a K+R vs K endgame. Black's king is centralized but must avoid the c-file (controlled by the white rook on c4) and stay out of check. Moving to e6 keeps the king active, stays off the edge, and doesn't walk into immediate opposition or checks from the white king on d4. Other options like d7d8 or d7e8 retreat toward the back rank (worse), while d7d6 is also reasonable but slightly closer to the white pieces. e6 is a standard "stay centralized" choice.
